country_event = {
	id = int.0
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		USA = {
			add_stability = -0.5
		}
		975 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = Cof_state_red_black_market scope = THIS.id } }
	} 
}

				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_artillery } }
					has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 1000 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_armor } }
					has_equipment = { medium_tank_chassis > 250 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects < 2
			}
		}

		add_timed_idea = { idea = Cof_weapons_payment_factory days = 120 }
		
		if = {
			limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_infantry } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 2500
					producer = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_artillery } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = 1000
					producer = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_armor } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_tank_chassis
					amount = 250
					producer = FRA
				}
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = weapons_trade_receive
		hidden_effect = { FRA = { country_event = cofintern.4 } }
	}	
	option = {
		name = cofintern.3.c
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					aluminium > 10
					chromium > 10
					oil > 10
					rubber > 10
					steel > 10
					tungsten > 10
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_infantry } }
					has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 2500 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_artillery } }
					has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 1000 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_armor } }
					has_equipment = { medium_tank_chassis > 250 }
				}
			}
		}

		random_core_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					aluminium > 10
					chromium > 10
					oil > 10
					rubber > 10
					steel > 10
					tungsten > 10
				}
			}
			set_state_flag = FRA_resource_rights
			THIS = { owner = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = FRA state = PREV.id } } }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = Cof_weapons_payment_resource days = 120 } 
		
		if = {
			limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_infantry } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 2500
					producer = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_artillery } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = 1000
					producer = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FRA = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_armor } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_tank_chassis
					amount = 250
					producer = FRA
				}
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = weapons_trade_receive
		hidden_effect = { FRA = { country_event = cofintern.4 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = cofintern.3.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = { FRA = { country_event = cofintern.4 } }

			}

		}
	}

		name = cofintern.4.b
		trigger = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = weapons_trade_receive } } }
		
	}

country_event = {
	id = cofintern.13
	title = cofintern.13.title
	desc = cofintern.13.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = cofintern.13.a
		add_stability = -0.025
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.01 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.025 }
	
		set_temp_variable = { t = var:THIS.party_popularity@totalist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { t = var:THIS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { t = var:THIS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { t = 20 }
		round_temp_variable = t

		set_temp_variable = { tt = 0.6 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { tt = THIS.stability }
		multiply_temp_variable = { tt = 10 }
		round_temp_variable = tt

		add_to_temp_variable = { t = tt }

		set_temp_variable = { bsg_civilian_factory_use = t }
		
		set_temp_variable = { rt = t }
		multiply_temp_variable = { rt = 3 }
		
		if = {
			limit = { aluminium > rt }
			set_temp_variable = { bsg_aluminium = rt }
		}
		else = { set_temp_variable = { bsg_aluminium = THIS.resource_produced@aluminium } }
		if = {
			limit = { chromium > rt }
			set_temp_variable = { bsg_chromium = rt }
		}
		else = { set_temp_variable = { bsg_chromium = THIS.resource_produced@chromium } }
		if = {
			limit = { oil > rt }
			set_temp_variable = { bsg_oil = rt }
		}
		else = { set_temp_variable = { bsg_oil = THIS.resource_produced@oil } }
		if = {
			limit = { rubber > rt }
			set_temp_variable = { bsg_rubber = rt }
		}
		else = { set_temp_variable = { bsg_rubber = THIS.resource_produced@rubber } }
		if = {
			limit = { steel > rt }
			set_temp_variable = { bsg_steel = rt }
		}
		else = { set_temp_variable = { bsg_steel = THIS.resource_produced@steel } }
		if = {
			limit = { tungsten > rt }
			set_temp_variable = { bsg_tungsten = rt }
		}
		else = { set_temp_variable = { bsg_tungsten = THIS.resource_produced@tungsten } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bsg_aluminium = -1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bsg_chromium = -1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bsg_oil = -1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bsg_rubber = -1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bsg_steel = -1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bsg_tungsten = -1 }

		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = Cof_border_smuggling_ger days = 90 }
	}
}

					has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_011

		}
	}

		text = cofintern.45.title.b
		trigger = {

				NOT = { has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_100 }

				NOT = { has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_101 }

			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = cofintern.45.desc.a
		trigger = {

			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = cofintern.45.a
		trigger = {
			RUS = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_100
					has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_010
					has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_001
					has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_110
					has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_101
					has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_011

				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_100 } }
			if = {
				limit = { tag = FRA }
				custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy
				set_temp_variable = { evc = 10 }
				cof_econ_target_change = yes
			}

			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			add_ideas = Cof_rus_cooperation_100

				limit = { tag = FRA }
				custom_effect_tooltip = effect_military
				set_temp_variable = { atc = 3 }
				set_temp_variable = { apc = 3 }

			}

				iri_influence_change = yes

			add_ideas = Cof_rus_cooperation_001
		}

			limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_110 } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy
				set_temp_variable = { evc = 10 }
				cof_econ_target_change = yes

				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = effect_military
				set_temp_variable = { atc = 3 }
				set_temp_variable = { apc = 3 }
				Cof_army_reform_values_change = yes
			}

			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			army_experience = 25
			add_ideas = Cof_rus_cooperation_110
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = rus_accept_cop_101 } }
			if = {
				limit = { tag = FRA }
				custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy
				set_temp_variable = { evc = 10 }
				cof_econ_target_change = yes

				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = effect_internation
				set_temp_variable = { iri_euic = 60 }

			}

			add_political_power = 100

		}
		else_if = {

				set_temp_variable = { apc = 3 }

			}

			army_experience = 25
			add_political_power = 100
			add_ideas = Cof_rus_cooperation_011
		}
		else_if = {

				custom_effect_tooltip = effect_economy

				}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = cofintern.87.a 
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject_of = GER }
			GER = { end_puppet = WAL }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FRA } }
			leave_faction = yes
		}

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.15 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.2 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.1 }
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:totalist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		FRA = { add_to_faction = WAL }
		set_stability = 0.8
		set_war_support = 0.5
		hidden_effect = {
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = WAL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = WAL_Hold_On_To_The_Monarchy
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = WAL_The_Government_Has_Failed
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = WAL_German_Investements
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = WAL_Retain_German_Staff
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = wallonia_events.112 days = 7 } }
		}
		complete_national_focus = WAL_Syndicalist_Revolution
		complete_national_focus = WAL_Revolution_By_Force
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = cofintern.115
	title = cofintern.115.title
	desc = {
		text = cofintern.115.desc.a
		trigger = { tag = FRA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = cofintern.115.desc.b
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = FRA } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { tag = FRA }
				FLA = { exists = yes } 
			}
			FLA = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = radical_socialist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.15 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.2 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.25 }
				complete_national_focus = FLA_Regency_By_The_Flemish_Council
				complete_national_focus = FLA_Syndicalist_Revolution
				FRA = { add_to_faction = WAL }
			}
		}

country_event = {
	id = int.1
	title = int.1.title
	desc = int.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = int.1.a
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		set_country_flag = phalanstere_attitude_agree 
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.phalanstere_vote_agree
			value = THIS.id
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = int.1.b
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		set_country_flag = phalanstere_attitude_oppose
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.phalanstere_vote_oppose
			value = THIS.id
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = int.1.c
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		set_country_flag = phalanstere_attitude_waiver 
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.phalanstere_vote_waiver
			value = THIS.id
		}
	}
}

	id = int.2
	title = int.2.title
	desc = int.2.desc

				limit = { FRA_is_phalanstere_member = yes }

			}
		}

	option = {

country_event = {
	id = int.3
	title = {
		text = int.3.title.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.phalanstere_vote_agree^num > global.phalanstere_vote_oppose^num } }
	}
	title = {
		text = int.3.title.b
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.phalanstere_vote_agree^num > global.phalanstere_vote_oppose^num } } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = int.3.desc.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.phalanstere_vote_agree^num > global.phalanstere_vote_oppose^num } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = int.3.desc.b
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.phalanstere_vote_agree^num > global.phalanstere_vote_oppose^num } } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	after = { 
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_array = global.phalanstere_vote_agree
			clear_array = global.phalanstere_vote_oppose
			clear_array = global.phalanstere_vote_waiver
			every_country = {
				limit = { FRA_is_phalanstere_member = yes }
				clr_country_flag = phalanstere_attitude_agree
				clr_country_flag = phalanstere_attitude_oppose
				clr_country_flag = phalanstere_attitude_waiver
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = int.3.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.phalanstere_vote_agree^num > global.phalanstere_vote_oppose^num } }
		phalanstere_vote_judge_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = int.3.b
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.phalanstere_vote_agree^num > global.phalanstere_vote_oppose^num } } }
		phalanstere_vote_judge_effect = yes
	}
}

		name = cofstory.1.b
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_stability = 0.005

		set_country_flag = Amir_worker

		ai_chance = { base = 50 }

		set_temp_variable = { pop_syndc = -0.1 }

		set_temp_variable = { pop_sorec = -0.1 }

		set_country_flag = Amir_local
	}	
}
